<ukm:Metadata xmlns:dc="http://purl.org/dc/elements/1.1/" xmlns:dct="http://purl.org/dc/terms/" xmlns:atom="http://www.w3.org/2005/Atom" xmlns:ukm="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/namespaces/metadata">
<dc:identifier>http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312</dc:identifier>
<dc:title>The Maternity and Parental Leave etc. Regulations 1999</dc:title>
<dc:type>text</dc:type>
<dc:format>text/xml</dc:format>
<dc:language>en</dc:language>
<dc:publisher>Statute Law Database</dc:publisher>
<dc:subject scheme="SIheading">TERMS AND CONDITIONS OF EMPLOYMENT</dc:subject>
<dc:modified>2025-04-24</dc:modified>
<dc:contributor>Expert Participation</dc:contributor>
<dct:valid>2025-04-06</dct:valid>
<dc:description>These Regulations, together with provisions inserted into the Employment Rights Act 1996 (“the 1996 Act") by the Employment Relations Act 1999, confer new rights to maternity and parental leave. The provisions relating to parental leave implement Council Directive 96/34/EC on the framework agreement on parental leave (OJ No.L145, 19.6.96, p.4).</dc:description>

<SecondaryPrelims DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/introduction" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/introduction" RestrictStartDate="1999-12-15">
<Number>1999 No. 3312</Number>
<SubjectInformation>
<Subject>
<Title>TERMS AND CONDITIONS OF EMPLOYMENT</Title>
</Subject>
</SubjectInformation>
<Title>The Maternity and Parental Leave etc. Regulations 1999</Title>
<MadeDate>
<Text> Made</Text>
<DateText>10th December 1999</DateText>
</MadeDate>
<ComingIntoForce>
<Text> Coming into force</Text>
<DateText>15th December 1999</DateText>
</ComingIntoForce>
<SecondaryPreamble>
<EnactingText>
<Para>
<Text>
Whereas a draft of the following Regulations was laid before Parliament in accordance with section 236(3) of the Employment Rights Act 1996
<CommentaryRef Ref="c16499841"/>
and approved by a resolution of each House of Parliament:
</Text>
</Para>
<Para>
<Text>
Now, therefore, the Secretary of State, in exercise of the powers conferred on him by sections 47C(2) and (3), 71(1) to (3) and (6), 72(1) and (2), 73(1), (2), (4) and (7), 74(1), (3) and (4), 75(1), 76(1), (2) and (5), 77(1) and (4), 78(1), (2) and (7), 79(1) and (2) and 99(1)
<CommentaryRef Ref="c16499851"/>
of that Act and of all other powers enabling him in that behalf, hereby makes the following Regulations:—
</Text>
</Para>
</EnactingText>
</SecondaryPreamble>
</SecondaryPrelims>
<Body DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/body" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/body" NumberOfProvisions="25" RestrictStartDate="2025-04-06">
<Part DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/part/1" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/part/1" NumberOfProvisions="3" id="part-1" RestrictStartDate="2013-04-08">
<Number>PART 1</Number>
<Title> GENERAL</Title>
<P1group RestrictStartDate="1999-12-15">
<Title> Citation and commencement</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/1" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/1" id="regulation-1">
<Pnumber>1</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<Text>These Regulations may be cited as the Maternity and Parental Leave etc. Regulations 1999 and shall come into force on 15th December 1999.</Text>
</P1para>
</P1>
</P1group>
<P1group RestrictStartDate="2013-04-08">
<Title> Interpretation</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2" id="regulation-2">
<Pnumber>2</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/1" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/1" id="regulation-2-1">
<Pnumber>1</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>In these Regulations—</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<UnorderedList Decoration="none">
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>“the 1996 Act" means the Employment Rights Act 1996;</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-c695762c6d2ece33c49aa7e2740f43c3-1670013027710" CommentaryRef="key-c695762c6d2ece33c49aa7e2740f43c3">"additional adoption leave" means leave under section 75B of the 1996 Act;</Addition>
</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>“additional maternity leave" means leave under section 73 of the 1996 Act;</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-1ba698ed803733261b283e15fb9d7efc-1670020256667" CommentaryRef="key-1ba698ed803733261b283e15fb9d7efc">“armed forces independence payment’’ means armed forces independence payment under the Armed Forces and Reserve Forces (Compensation Scheme) Order 2011;</Addition>
</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>“business" includes a trade or profession and includes any activity carried on by a body of persons (whether corporate or unincorporated);</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>“child" means a person under the age of eighteen;</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>“childbirth" means the birth of a living child or the birth of a child whether living or dead after 24 weeks of pregnancy;</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>
“collective agreement" means a collective agreement within the meaning of section 178 of the Trade Union and Labour Relations (Consolidation) Act 1992
<CommentaryRef Ref="c16499861"/>
, the trade union parties to which are independent trade unions within the meaning of section 5 of that Act;
</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>“contract of employment" means a contract of service or apprenticeship, whether express or implied, and (if it is express) whether oral or in writing;</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>
“disability living allowance" means the disability living allowance provided for in Part III of the Social Security Contributions and Benefits Act 1992
<CommentaryRef Ref="c16499871"/>
;
</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>“employee" means an individual who has entered into or works under (or, where the employment has ceased, worked under) a contract of employment;</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>“employer" means the person by whom an employee is (or, where the employment has ceased, was) employed;</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>“expected week of childbirth" means the week, beginning with midnight between Saturday and Sunday, in which it is expected that childbirth will occur, and “week of childbirth" means the week, beginning with midnight between Saturday and Sunday, in which childbirth occurs;</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>
“job", in relation to an employee returning after
<CommentaryRef Ref="key-bb5af1b361a7773b0ac97038cf34f568"/>
... maternity leave or parental leave, means the nature of the work which she is employed to do in accordance with her contract and the capacity and place in which she is so employed;
</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>“ordinary maternity leave" means leave under section 71 of the 1996 Act;</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>“parental leave" means leave under regulation 13(1);</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>
“parental responsibility" has the meaning given by section 3 of the Children Act 1989
<CommentaryRef Ref="c16499881"/>
, and “parental responsibilities" has the meaning given by section 1(3) of the Children (Scotland) Act 1995
<CommentaryRef Ref="c16499891"/>
;
</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-70b8d839b9e93e2a3bba56435ee77003-1670020303237" CommentaryRef="key-70b8d839b9e93e2a3bba56435ee77003">“personal independence payment” means personal independence payment under Part 4 of the Welfare Reform Act 2012;</Addition>
</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-c328502e290513595fe14bb384fdb3ae-1670013123093" CommentaryRef="key-c328502e290513595fe14bb384fdb3ae">"statutory leave" means leave provided for in Part 8 of the 1996 Act;</Addition>
</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-f056cc325feeb0358d2129946585e994-1670015437635" CommentaryRef="key-f056cc325feeb0358d2129946585e994">“statutory maternity leave” means ordinary maternity leave and additional maternity leave;</Addition>
</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-f056cc325feeb0358d2129946585e994-1670015437635" CommentaryRef="key-f056cc325feeb0358d2129946585e994">“statutory maternity leave period” means the period during which the employee is on statutory maternity leave;</Addition>
</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
<ListItem>
<Para>
<Text>“workforce agreement" means an agreement between an employer and his employees or their representatives in respect of which the conditions set out in Schedule 1 to these Regulations are satisfied.</Text>
</Para>
</ListItem>
</UnorderedList>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/2" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/2" id="regulation-2-2">
<Pnumber>2</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>A reference in any provision of these Regulations to a period of continuous employment is to a period computed in accordance with Chapter I of Part XIV of the 1996 Act, as if that provision were a provision of that Act.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/3" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/3" id="regulation-2-3">
<Pnumber>3</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>For the purposes of these Regulations any two employers shall be treated as associated if—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/3/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/3/a" id="regulation-2-3-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>one is a company of which the other (directly or indirectly) has control; or</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/3/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/3/b" id="regulation-2-3-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>both are companies of which a third person (directly or indirectly) has control;</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<Text>and “associated employer" shall be construed accordingly.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/4" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/4" id="regulation-2-4">
<Pnumber>4</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>In these Regulations, unless the context otherwise requires,—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/4/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/4/a" id="regulation-2-4-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>a reference to a numbered regulation or schedule is to the regulation or schedule in these Regulations bearing that number;</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/4/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/4/b" id="regulation-2-4-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>a reference in a regulation or schedule to a numbered paragraph is to the paragraph in that regulation or schedule bearing that number, and</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/4/c" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/2/4/c" id="regulation-2-4-c">
<Pnumber>c</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>a reference in a paragraph to a lettered sub-paragraph is to the sub-paragraph in that paragraph bearing that letter.</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P2para>
</P2>
</P1para>
</P1>
</P1group>
<P1group RestrictStartDate="1999-12-15">
<Title> Application</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3" id="regulation-3">
<Pnumber>3</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/1" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/1" id="regulation-3-1">
<Pnumber>1</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>The provisions of Part II of these Regulations have effect only in relation to employees whose expected week of childbirth begins on or after 30th April 2000.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/2" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/2" id="regulation-3-2">
<Pnumber>2</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>Regulation 19 (protection from detriment) has effect only in relation to an act or failure to act which takes place on or after 15th December 1999.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/3" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/3" id="regulation-3-3">
<Pnumber>3</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>For the purposes of paragraph (2)—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/3/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/3/a" id="regulation-3-3-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>where an act extends over a period, the reference to the date of the act is a reference to the last day of that period, and</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/3/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/3/b" id="regulation-3-3-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>a failure to act is to be treated as done when it was decided on.</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/4" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/4" id="regulation-3-4">
<Pnumber>4</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>For the purposes of paragraph (3), in the absence of evidence establishing the contrary an employer shall be taken to decide on a failure to act—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/4/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/4/a" id="regulation-3-4-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>when he does an act inconsistent with doing the failed act, or</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/4/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/4/b" id="regulation-3-4-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>if he has done no such inconsistent act, when the period expires within which he might reasonably have been expected to do the failed act if it was to be done.</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/5" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/3/5" id="regulation-3-5">
<Pnumber>5</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>Regulation 20 (unfair dismissal) has effect only in relation to dismissals where the effective date of termination (within the meaning of section 97 of the 1996 Act) falls on or after 15th December 1999.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
</P1para>
</P1>
</P1group>
</Part>

<Title>
Entitlement to ordinary maternity leave
<Addition ChangeId="key-8b2ddce721be12ae86553f7240e0c5ab-1670015596596" CommentaryRef="key-8b2ddce721be12ae86553f7240e0c5ab">and to additional maternity leave</Addition>
</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4" id="regulation-4">
<Pnumber>4</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1" id="regulation-4-1">
<Pnumber>1</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>
An employee is entitled to ordinary maternity leave
<Addition ChangeId="key-ec4cd43b87ca77ca079bfcbdf762e353-1670015638756" CommentaryRef="key-ec4cd43b87ca77ca079bfcbdf762e353">and to additional maternity leave</Addition>
provided that she satisfies the following conditions—
</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/a" id="regulation-4-1-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>
<Substitution ChangeId="key-1be3a539dc0fe4f8a1e171480a36fb59-1670013307394" CommentaryRef="key-1be3a539dc0fe4f8a1e171480a36fb59">no later than the end of the fifteenth week before her expected week of childbirth</Substitution>
, or, if that is not reasonably practicable, as soon as is reasonably practicable, she notifies her employer of—
</Text>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/a/i" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/a/i" id="regulation-4-1-a-i">
<Pnumber>i</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>her pregnancy;</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/a/ii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/a/ii" id="regulation-4-1-a-ii">
<Pnumber>ii</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>the expected week of childbirth, and</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/a/iii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/a/iii" id="regulation-4-1-a-iii">
<Pnumber>iii</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>the date on which she intends her ordinary maternity leave period to start,</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<Text>and</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/b" id="regulation-4-1-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>if requested to do so by her employer, she produces for his inspection a certificate from—</Text>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/b/i" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/b/i" id="regulation-4-1-b-i">
<Pnumber>i</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>a registered medical practitioner, or</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/b/ii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/1/b/ii" id="regulation-4-1-b-ii">
<Pnumber>ii</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>a registered midwife,</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<Text>stating the expected week of childbirth.</Text>

</P2para>

—

<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/3" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/3" id="regulation-4-3">

before the expected week of childbirth on which she is absent from work wholly or partly because of pregnancy—

<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/3/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/4/3/a" id="regulation-4-3-a">

.

.

<Title> Commencement of maternity leave periods</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/6" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/6" id="regulation-6">
<Pnumber>6</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/6/1" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/6/1" id="regulation-6-1">
<Pnumber>1</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>Subject to paragraph (2), an employee’s ordinary maternity leave period commences with the earlier of—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/6/1/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/6/1/a" id="regulation-6-1-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>
the date which
<CommentaryRef Ref="key-d81c8e23cffc7d50c078ebc49cc15d78"/>
... she notifies to her employer
<Addition ChangeId="key-643060dc723603f76984ad9932bca139-1670013950025" CommentaryRef="key-643060dc723603f76984ad9932bca139">, in accordance with regulation 4,</Addition>
as the date on which she intends her ordinary maternity leave period to start,
<Addition ChangeId="key-0fd73fdbce070b777f08059f0f963594-1670013985101" CommentaryRef="key-0fd73fdbce070b777f08059f0f963594">or, if by virtue of the provision for variation in that regulation she has notified more than one such date, the last date she notifies,</Addition>
and
</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/6/1/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/6/1/b" id="regulation-6-1-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-5429b8750d88e3d68f4810702ca4bc88-1670014035108" CommentaryRef="key-5429b8750d88e3d68f4810702ca4bc88">the day which follows</Addition>
the first day after the beginning of
<Substitution ChangeId="key-aac0113edf6bfd12da7fec32a7fd1966-1670014098676" CommentaryRef="key-aac0113edf6bfd12da7fec32a7fd1966">the fourth week</Substitution>
before the expected week of childbirth on which she is absent from work wholly or partly because of pregnancy.
</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/6/2" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/6/2" id="regulation-6-2">
<Pnumber>2</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>
Where the employee’s ordinary maternity leave period has not commenced by virtue of paragraph (1) when childbirth occurs, her ordinary maternity leave period commences
<Substitution ChangeId="key-80bf7b384d62355aab95a5ef4909ccd3-1670014137029" CommentaryRef="key-80bf7b384d62355aab95a5ef4909ccd3">on the day which follows</Substitution>
the day on which childbirth occurs.
</Text>
</P2para>

<Pnumber>3</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>An employee’s additional maternity leave period commences on the day after the last day of her ordinary maternity leave period.</Text>
</P2para>

<P1group RestrictStartDate="2006-10-01">
<Title> Duration of maternity leave periods</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/7" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/7" id="regulation-7">
<Pnumber>7</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/7/1" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/7/1" id="regulation-7-1">
<Pnumber>1</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>
Subject to paragraphs (2) and (5), an employee’s ordinary maternity leave period continues for the period of
<Substitution ChangeId="key-c5655b808b7909096770b18004f5a719-1670014266241" CommentaryRef="key-c5655b808b7909096770b18004f5a719">26 weeks</Substitution>
from its commencement, or until the end of the compulsory maternity leave period provided for in regulation 8 if later.
</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/7/2" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/7/2" id="regulation-7-2">
<Pnumber>2</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>Subject to paragraph (5), where any requirement imposed by or under any relevant statutory provision prohibits the employee from working for any period after the end of the period determined under paragraph (1) by reason of her having recently given birth, her ordinary maternity leave period continues until the end of that later period.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>

<Pnumber>3</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>In paragraph (2), “relevant statutory provision" means a provision of—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/7/3/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/7/3/a" id="regulation-7-3-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>an enactment, or</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>

<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>an instrument under an enactment,</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<Text>other than a provision for the time being specified in an order under section 66(2) of the 1996 Act.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/7/4" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/7/4" id="regulation-7-4">
<Pnumber>4</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>
Subject to paragraph (5), where an employee is entitled to additional maternity leave her additional maternity leave period continues until the end of the period of
<Substitution ChangeId="key-61554a10165e187d125239f0ac47520b-1670014309268" CommentaryRef="key-61554a10165e187d125239f0ac47520b">26 weeks from the day on which it commenced</Substitution>

<Pnumber>5</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>Where the employee is dismissed after the commencement of an ordinary or additional maternity leave period but before the time when (apart from this paragraph) that period would end, the period ends at the time of the dismissal.</Text>

<Title> Compulsory maternity leave</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/8" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/8" id="regulation-8">
<Pnumber>8</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<Text>The prohibition in section 72 of the 1996 Act, against permitting an employee who satisfies prescribed conditions to work during a particular period (referred to as a “compulsory maternity leave period"), applies—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/8/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/8/a" id="regulation-8-a">

<P3para>

<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>in respect of the period of two weeks which commences with the day on which childbirth occurs.</Text>

<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>

<Pnumber>4</Pnumber>

<P2para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e-1670015192198" CommentaryRef="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e">Subject to paragraph (4), for the purposes of this regulation, work means any work done under the contract of employment and may include training or any activity undertaken for the purposes of keeping in touch with the workplace.</Addition>
</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/12A/4" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/12A/4" id="regulation-12A-4">
<Pnumber>
<Addition ChangeId="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e-1670015192198" CommentaryRef="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e">4</Addition>
</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e-1670015192198" CommentaryRef="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e">Reasonable contact from time to time between an employee and her employer which either party is entitled to make during a maternity leave period (for example to discuss an employee’s return to work) shall not bring that period to an end.</Addition>
</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/12A/5" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/12A/5" id="regulation-12A-5">
<Pnumber>
<Addition ChangeId="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e-1670015192198" CommentaryRef="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e">5</Addition>
</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e-1670015192198" CommentaryRef="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e">Paragraph (1) shall not apply in relation to any work carried out by the employee at any time from childbirth to the end of the period of two weeks which commences with the day on which childbirth occurs.</Addition>
</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/12A/6" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/12A/6" id="regulation-12A-6">
<Pnumber>
<Addition ChangeId="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e-1670015192198" CommentaryRef="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e">6</Addition>
</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e-1670015192198" CommentaryRef="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e">This regulation does not confer any right on an employer to require that any work be carried out during the statutory maternity leave period, nor any right on an employee to work during the statutory maternity leave period.</Addition>
</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/12A/7" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/12A/7" id="regulation-12A-7">
<Pnumber>
<Addition ChangeId="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e-1670015192198" CommentaryRef="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e">7</Addition>

<Addition ChangeId="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e-1670015192198" CommentaryRef="key-fbe3ffc9e46851b2d7363f424b00498e">Any days' work carried out under this regulation shall not have the effect of extending the total duration of the statutory maternity leave period.</Addition>
</Text>
</P2para>

<Part DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/part/III" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/part/III" NumberOfProvisions="5" id="part-III" RestrictStartDate="2015-04-05">
<Number>PART III</Number>
<Title> PARENTAL LEAVE</Title>
<P1group RestrictStartDate="2015-04-05">
<Title> Entitlement to parental leave</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13" id="regulation-13">
<Pnumber>13</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/1" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/1" id="regulation-13-1">
<Pnumber>1</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>An employee who—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/1/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/1/a" id="regulation-13-1-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>
has been continuously employed for a period of not less than a year
<Addition ChangeId="key-caeaec9b01c15d44ba63bd8c0cafcf18-1670011957175" CommentaryRef="key-caeaec9b01c15d44ba63bd8c0cafcf18">or is to be treated as having been so employed by virtue of paragraph (1A)</Addition>
; and
</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/1/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/1/b" id="regulation-13-1-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>has, or expects to have, responsibility for a child,</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<Text>is entitled, in accordance with these Regulations, to be absent from work on parental leave for the purpose of caring for that child.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/1A" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/1A" id="regulation-13-1A">
<Pnumber>
<CommentaryRef Ref="key-a68c238af18489cab7496cdafb5d0d1a"/>
1A
</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>. . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . .</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/2" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/2" id="regulation-13-2">
<Pnumber>2</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>An employee has responsibility for a child, for the purposes of paragraph (1), if—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/2/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/2/a" id="regulation-13-2-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>he has parental responsibility or, in Scotland, parental responsibilities for the child; or</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/2/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/2/b" id="regulation-13-2-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>
he has been registered as the child’s father under any provision of section 10(1) or 10A(1) of the Births and Deaths Registration Act 1953
<CommentaryRef Ref="c16499901"/>
or of section 18(1) or (2) of the Registration of Births, Deaths and Marriages (Scotland) Act 1965
<CommentaryRef Ref="c16499911"/>
.
</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/3" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/13/3" id="regulation-13-3">
<Pnumber>
<CommentaryRef Ref="key-c9b08b16ea1338a6e9f54f53a1d25f28"/>
3
</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>. . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . .</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
</P1para>
</P1>
</P1group>
<P1group RestrictStartDate="2013-03-08">
<Title> Extent of entitlement</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/14" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/14" id="regulation-14">
<Pnumber>14</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/14/1" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/14/1" id="regulation-14-1">
<Pnumber>
<Substitution ChangeId="key-1463a334012ab9c2a5220c839b505779-1670020101328" CommentaryRef="key-1463a334012ab9c2a5220c839b505779">1</Substitution>
</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>
<Substitution ChangeId="key-1463a334012ab9c2a5220c839b505779-1670020101328" CommentaryRef="key-1463a334012ab9c2a5220c839b505779">An employee is entitled to eighteen weeks’ leave in respect of any individual child.</Substitution>
</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/14/1A" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/14/1A" id="regulation-14-1A">
<Pnumber>
<CommentaryRef Ref="key-7999531ccf31f9df95a728a66ad838aa"/>
1A
</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>. . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . .</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/14/2" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/14/2" id="regulation-14-2">
<Pnumber>2</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>Where the period for which an employee is normally required, under his contract of employment, to work in the course of a week does not vary, a week’s leave for the employee is a period of absence from work which is equal in duration to the period for which he is normally required to work.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/14/3" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/14/3" id="regulation-14-3">
<Pnumber>3</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>Where the period for which an employee is normally required, under his contract of employment, to work in the course of a week varies from week to week or over a longer period, or where he is normally required under his contract to work in some weeks but not in others, a week’s leave for the employee is a period of absence from work which is equal in duration to the period calculated by dividing the total of the periods for which he is normally required to work in a year by 52.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/14/4" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/14/4" id="regulation-14-4">
<Pnumber>4</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>Where an employee takes leave in periods shorter than the period which constitutes, for him, a week’s leave under whichever of paragraphs (2) and (3) is applicable in his case, he completes a week’s leave when the aggregate of the periods of leave he has taken equals the period constituting a week’s leave for him under the applicable paragraph.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
</P1para>
</P1>
</P1group>
<P1group RestrictStartDate="2015-04-05">
<Title> When parental leave may be taken</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/15" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/15" id="regulation-15">
<Pnumber>
<Substitution ChangeId="key-58edfe73b43c27ac92b3b7ec080236da-1670021495443" CommentaryRef="key-58edfe73b43c27ac92b3b7ec080236da">15</Substitution>
</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<Text>
<Substitution ChangeId="key-58edfe73b43c27ac92b3b7ec080236da-1670021495443" CommentaryRef="key-58edfe73b43c27ac92b3b7ec080236da">An employee may not exercise any entitlement to parental leave in respect of a child after the date of the child’s 18th birthday.</Substitution>
</Text>
</P1para>
</P1>
</P1group>
<P1group RestrictStartDate="1999-12-15">
<Title> Default provisions in respect of parental leave</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/16" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/16" id="regulation-16">
<Pnumber>16</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<Text>The provisions set out in Schedule 2 apply in relation to parental leave in the case of an employee whose contract of employment does not include a provision which—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/16/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/16/a" id="regulation-16-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>confers an entitlement to absence from work for the purpose of caring for a child, and</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/16/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/16/b" id="regulation-16-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>incorporates or operates by reference to all or part of a collective agreement or workforce agreement.</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P1para>
</P1>
</P1group>
<P1group RestrictStartDate="2013-03-08">

<Number>PART IV</Number>
<Title> PROVISIONS APPLICABLE IN RELATION TO MORE THAN ONE KIND OF ABSENCE</Title>
<P1group RestrictStartDate="2008-07-23">
<Title> Application of terms and conditions during periods of leave</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17" id="regulation-17">
<Pnumber>17</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<Text>
An employee who takes
<CommentaryRef Ref="key-6bbce73a37b1c1bf8f7d4f5593da9b36"/>
... parental leave—
</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/a" id="regulation-17-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>is entitled, during the period of leave, to the benefit of her employer’s implied obligation to her of trust and confidence and any terms and conditions of her employment relating to—</Text>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/a/i" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/a/i" id="regulation-17-a-i">
<Pnumber>i</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>notice of the termination of the employment contract by her employer;</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/a/ii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/a/ii" id="regulation-17-a-ii">
<Pnumber>ii</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>compensation in the event of redundancy, or</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/a/iii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/a/iii" id="regulation-17-a-iii">
<Pnumber>iii</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>disciplinary or grievance procedures;</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/b" id="regulation-17-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>is bound, during that period, by her implied obligation to her employer of good faith and any terms and conditions of her employment relating to—</Text>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/b/i" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/b/i" id="regulation-17-b-i">
<Pnumber>i</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>notice of the termination of the employment contract by her;</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/b/ii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/b/ii" id="regulation-17-b-ii">
<Pnumber>ii</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>the disclosure of confidential information;</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/b/iii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/b/iii" id="regulation-17-b-iii">
<Pnumber>iii</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>the acceptance of gifts or other benefits, or</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/b/iv" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/17/b/iv" id="regulation-17-b-iv">
<Pnumber>iv</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>the employee’s participation in any other business.</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P1para>

<P1group RestrictStartDate="2008-07-23">
<Title> Protection from detriment</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19" id="regulation-19">
<Pnumber>19</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/1" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/1" id="regulation-19-1">
<Pnumber>1</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>An employee is entitled under section 47C of the 1996 Act not to be subjected to any detriment by any act, or any deliberate failure to act, by her employer done for any of the reasons specified in paragraph (2).</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2" id="regulation-19-2">
<Pnumber>2</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>The reasons referred to in paragraph (1) are that the employee—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/a" id="regulation-19-2-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>is pregnant;</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/b" id="regulation-19-2-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>has given birth to a child;</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/c" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/c" id="regulation-19-2-c">
<Pnumber>c</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>is the subject of a relevant requirement, or a relevant recommendation, as defined by section 66(2) of the 1996 Act;</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/d" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/d" id="regulation-19-2-d">
<Pnumber>d</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>
took, sought to take or availed herself of the benefits of, ordinary maternity leave
<Addition ChangeId="key-7a8b91639f6ffaadfe6d25c4b3b06dd1-1670019726151" CommentaryRef="key-7a8b91639f6ffaadfe6d25c4b3b06dd1">or additional maternity leave</Addition>
;
</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/e" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/e" id="regulation-19-2-e">
<Pnumber>e</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>took or sought to take—</Text>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/e/i" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/e/i" id="regulation-19-2-e-i">
<Pnumber>
<CommentaryRef Ref="key-91eecdcb2dde64e8f02effc0cf45bf41"/>
i
</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>. . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . .</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/e/ii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/e/ii" id="regulation-19-2-e-ii">
<Pnumber>ii</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>parental leave, or</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/e/iii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/e/iii" id="regulation-19-2-e-iii">
<Pnumber>iii</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>time off under section 57A of the 1996 Act;</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/ee" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/ee" id="regulation-19-2-ee">
<Pnumber>
<Addition ChangeId="key-4c9083f1da0ceb7856079dd4f6ea8593-1670014895731" CommentaryRef="key-4c9083f1da0ceb7856079dd4f6ea8593">ee</Addition>
</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-4c9083f1da0ceb7856079dd4f6ea8593-1670014895731" CommentaryRef="key-4c9083f1da0ceb7856079dd4f6ea8593">failed to return after a period of ordinary or additional maternity leave in a case where—</Addition>
</Text>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/ee/i" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/ee/i" id="regulation-19-2-ee-i">
<Pnumber>
<Addition ChangeId="key-4c9083f1da0ceb7856079dd4f6ea8593-1670014895731" CommentaryRef="key-4c9083f1da0ceb7856079dd4f6ea8593">i</Addition>
</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-4c9083f1da0ceb7856079dd4f6ea8593-1670014895731" CommentaryRef="key-4c9083f1da0ceb7856079dd4f6ea8593">the employer did not notify her, in accordance with regulation 7(6) and (7) or otherwise, of the date on which the period in question would end, and she reasonably believed that that period had not ended, or</Addition>
</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/ee/ii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/ee/ii" id="regulation-19-2-ee-ii">
<Pnumber>
<Addition ChangeId="key-4c9083f1da0ceb7856079dd4f6ea8593-1670014895731" CommentaryRef="key-4c9083f1da0ceb7856079dd4f6ea8593">ii</Addition>
</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-4c9083f1da0ceb7856079dd4f6ea8593-1670014895731" CommentaryRef="key-4c9083f1da0ceb7856079dd4f6ea8593">the employer gave her less than 28 days' notice of the date on which the period in question would end, and it was not reasonably practicable for her to return on that date;</Addition>
</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/eee" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/eee" id="regulation-19-2-eee">
<Pnumber>
<Addition ChangeId="key-6f579ca9275a28cd41f19bf26c25ede0-1670018668071" CommentaryRef="key-6f579ca9275a28cd41f19bf26c25ede0">eee</Addition>
</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-6f579ca9275a28cd41f19bf26c25ede0-1670018668071" CommentaryRef="key-6f579ca9275a28cd41f19bf26c25ede0">undertook, considered undertaking or refused to undertake work in accordance with regulation 12A;</Addition>
</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/f" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/f" id="regulation-19-2-f">
<Pnumber>f</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>declined to sign a workforce agreement for the purpose of these Regulations, or</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/g" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/g" id="regulation-19-2-g">
<Pnumber>g</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>being—</Text>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/g/i" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/g/i" id="regulation-19-2-g-i">
<Pnumber>i</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>a representative of members of the workforce for the purposes of Schedule 1, or</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/g/ii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/2/g/ii" id="regulation-19-2-g-ii">
<Pnumber>ii</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>a candidate in an election in which any person elected will, on being elected, become such a representative,</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<Text>performed (or proposed to perform) any functions or activities as such a representative or candidate.</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/3" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/3" id="regulation-19-3">
<Pnumber>3</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>
For the purposes of paragraph (2)(d), a woman avails herself of the benefits of ordinary maternity leave if, during her ordinary maternity leave period, she avails herself of the benefit of any of the terms and conditions of her employment preserved by section 71 of the 1996 Act
<Addition ChangeId="key-d425156a6569598981673fd1fcba9053-1670014922337" CommentaryRef="key-d425156a6569598981673fd1fcba9053">and regulation 9</Addition>
during that period.
</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/3A" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/3A" id="regulation-19-3A">
<Pnumber>
<Addition ChangeId="key-f5eaee6ffd823ee1011e6dd9179437a6-1670019662838" CommentaryRef="key-f5eaee6ffd823ee1011e6dd9179437a6">3A</Addition>
</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-f5eaee6ffd823ee1011e6dd9179437a6-1670019662838" CommentaryRef="key-f5eaee6ffd823ee1011e6dd9179437a6">For the purposes of paragraph (2)(d), a woman avails herself of the benefits of additional maternity leave if, during her additional maternity leave period, she avails herself of the benefit of any of the terms and conditions of her employment preserved by section 73 of the 1996 Act and regulation 9 during that period.</Addition>
</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/4" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/4" id="regulation-19-4">
<Pnumber>4</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>Paragraph (1) does not apply in a case where the detriment in question amounts to dismissal within the meaning of Part X of the 1996 Act.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/5" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/5" id="regulation-19-5">
<Pnumber>5</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>Paragraph (2)(b) only applies where the act or failure to act takes place during the employee’s ordinary or additional maternity leave period.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/6" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/6" id="regulation-19-6">
<Pnumber>6</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>For the purposes of paragraph (5)—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/6/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/6/a" id="regulation-19-6-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>where an act extends over a period, the reference to the date of the act is a reference to the last day of that period, and</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/6/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/6/b" id="regulation-19-6-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>a failure to act is to be treated as done when it was decided on.</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/7" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/7" id="regulation-19-7">
<Pnumber>7</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>For the purposes of paragraph (6), in the absence of evidence establishing the contrary an employer shall be taken to decide on a failure to act—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/7/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/7/a" id="regulation-19-7-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>when he does an act inconsistent with doing the failed act, or</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/7/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/19/7/b" id="regulation-19-7-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>if he has done no such inconsistent act, when the period expires within which he might reasonably have been expected to do the failed act if it were to be done.</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P2para>
</P2>

<P1group RestrictStartDate="2025-04-06">
<Title> Unfair dismissal</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20" id="regulation-20">
<Pnumber>20</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/1" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/1" id="regulation-20-1">
<Pnumber>1</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>An employee who is dismissed is entitled under section 99 of the 1996 Act to be regarded for the purposes of Part X of that Act as unfairly dismissed if—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/1/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/1/a" id="regulation-20-1-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>the reason or principal reason for the dismissal is of a kind specified in paragraph (3), or</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/1/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/1/b" id="regulation-20-1-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>the reason or principal reason for the dismissal is that the employee is redundant, and regulation 10 has not been complied with.</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/2" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/2" id="regulation-20-2">
<Pnumber>2</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>An employee who is dismissed shall also be regarded for the purposes of Part X of the 1996 Act as unfairly dismissed if—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/2/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/2/a" id="regulation-20-2-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>the reason (or, if more than one, the principal reason) for the dismissal is that the employee was redundant;</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/2/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/2/b" id="regulation-20-2-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>it is shown that the circumstances constituting the redundancy applied equally to one or more employees in the same undertaking who held positions similar to that held by the employee and who have not been dismissed by the employer, and</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/2/c" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/2/c" id="regulation-20-2-c">
<Pnumber>c</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>it is shown that the reason (or, if more than one, the principal reason) for which the employee was selected for dismissal was a reason of a kind specified in paragraph (3).</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3" id="regulation-20-3">
<Pnumber>3</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>The kinds of reason referred to in paragraphs (1) and (2) are reasons connected with—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/a" id="regulation-20-3-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>the pregnancy of the employee;</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/b" id="regulation-20-3-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>the fact that the employee has given birth to a child;</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/c" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/c" id="regulation-20-3-c">
<Pnumber>c</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>the application of a relevant requirement, or a relevant recommendation, as defined by section 66(2) of the 1996 Act;</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/d" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/d" id="regulation-20-3-d">
<Pnumber>d</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>
the fact that she took, sought to take or availed herself of the benefits of, ordinary maternity leave
<Addition ChangeId="key-f672ff1a3bf65e2e29127dff58451f5e-1670019867037" CommentaryRef="key-f672ff1a3bf65e2e29127dff58451f5e">or additional maternity leave</Addition>
;
</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/e" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/e" id="regulation-20-3-e">
<Pnumber>e</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>the fact that she took or sought to take—</Text>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/e/i" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/e/i" id="regulation-20-3-e-i">
<Pnumber>
<CommentaryRef Ref="key-40ec76bf42c8bbabb9f34d94bd66fe35"/>
i
</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>. . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . .</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/e/ii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/e/ii" id="regulation-20-3-e-ii">
<Pnumber>ii</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>parental leave, or</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/e/iii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/e/iii" id="regulation-20-3-e-iii">
<Pnumber>iii</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>time off under section 57A of the 1996 Act;</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/ee" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/ee" id="regulation-20-3-ee">
<Pnumber>
<Addition ChangeId="key-f1c97aacd87b5170af35198ecbb95625-1670014988984" CommentaryRef="key-f1c97aacd87b5170af35198ecbb95625">ee</Addition>
</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-f1c97aacd87b5170af35198ecbb95625-1670014988984" CommentaryRef="key-f1c97aacd87b5170af35198ecbb95625">the fact that she failed to return after a period of ordinary or additional maternity leave in a case where—</Addition>
</Text>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/ee/i" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/ee/i" id="regulation-20-3-ee-i">
<Pnumber>
<Addition ChangeId="key-f1c97aacd87b5170af35198ecbb95625-1670014988984" CommentaryRef="key-f1c97aacd87b5170af35198ecbb95625">i</Addition>
</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-f1c97aacd87b5170af35198ecbb95625-1670014988984" CommentaryRef="key-f1c97aacd87b5170af35198ecbb95625">the employer did not notify her, in accordance with regulation 7(6) and (7) or otherwise, of the date on which the period in question would end, and she reasonably believed that that period had not ended, or</Addition>
</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/ee/ii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/ee/ii" id="regulation-20-3-ee-ii">
<Pnumber>
<Addition ChangeId="key-f1c97aacd87b5170af35198ecbb95625-1670014988984" CommentaryRef="key-f1c97aacd87b5170af35198ecbb95625">ii</Addition>
</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>
<Addition ChangeId="key-f1c97aacd87b5170af35198ecbb95625-1670014988984" CommentaryRef="key-f1c97aacd87b5170af35198ecbb95625">the employer gave her less than 28 days' notice of the date on which the period in question would end, and it was not reasonably practicable for her to return on that date;</Addition>
</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/eee" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/eee" id="regulation-20-3-eee">

<Addition ChangeId="key-bd3962fb586a875031c5285491a03552-1670018741617" CommentaryRef="key-bd3962fb586a875031c5285491a03552">the fact that she undertook, considered undertaking or refused to undertake work in accordance with regulation 12A;</Addition>
</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/f" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/f" id="regulation-20-3-f">
<Pnumber>f</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>the fact that she declined to sign a workforce agreement for the purposes of these Regulations, or</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/g" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/g" id="regulation-20-3-g">
<Pnumber>g</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>the fact that the employee, being—</Text>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/g/i" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/g/i" id="regulation-20-3-g-i">
<Pnumber>i</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>a representative of members of the workforce for the purposes of Schedule 1, or</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<P4 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/g/ii" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/3/g/ii" id="regulation-20-3-g-ii">
<Pnumber>ii</Pnumber>
<P4para>
<Text>a candidate in an election in which any person elected will, on being elected, become such a representative,</Text>
</P4para>
</P4>
<Text>performed (or proposed to perform) any functions or activities as such a representative or candidate.</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/4" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/4" id="regulation-20-4">
<Pnumber>4</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>
<Substitution ChangeId="key-80fafc0adbcb3f2c014ad2d3952e1f72-1745494890000" CommentaryRef="key-80fafc0adbcb3f2c014ad2d3952e1f72">Paragraph (3)(b) only applies</Substitution>
where the dismissal ends the employee’s ordinary or additional maternity leave period.
</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/5" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/5" id="regulation-20-5">
<Pnumber>

<P2para>
<Text>
<Substitution ChangeId="key-9fc44b1cb1c8623d698aff896697e63c-1670019809127" CommentaryRef="key-9fc44b1cb1c8623d698aff896697e63c">Paragraphs (3) and (3A) of regulation 19 apply for the purposes of paragraph (3)(d) as they apply for the purposes of paragraph (2)(d) of that regulation.</Substitution>

<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/6" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/6" id="regulation-20-6">
<Pnumber>
<CommentaryRef Ref="key-5fed48c64a1d8d3601721ac0db7bbf89"/>
6
</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>. . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . . .</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/7" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/7" id="regulation-20-7">
<Pnumber>7</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>Paragraph (1) does not apply in relation to an employee if—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/7/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/7/a" id="regulation-20-7-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>it is not reasonably practicable for a reason other than redundancy for the employer (who may be the same employer or a successor of his) to permit her to return to a job which is both suitable for her and appropriate for her to do in the circumstances;</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/7/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/7/b" id="regulation-20-7-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>an associated employer offers her a job of that kind, and</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/7/c" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/7/c" id="regulation-20-7-c">
<Pnumber>c</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>she accepts or unreasonably refuses that offer.</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/8" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/20/8" id="regulation-20-8">
<Pnumber>8</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>
Where on a complaint of unfair dismissal any question arises as to whether the operation of paragraph (1) is excluded by the provisions of paragraph
<CommentaryRef Ref="key-f193688020ec303abf46e9d605abcd5e"/>
... (7), it is for the employer to show that the provisions in question were satisfied in relation to the complainant.
</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
</P1para>

<P1group RestrictStartDate="1999-12-15">
<Title> Contractual rights to maternity or parental leave</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21" id="regulation-21">
<Pnumber>21</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/1" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/1" id="regulation-21-1">
<Pnumber>1</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>This regulation applies where an employee is entitled to—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/1/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/1/a" id="regulation-21-1-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>ordinary maternity leave;</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/1/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/1/b" id="regulation-21-1-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>additional maternity leave, or</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/1/c" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/1/c" id="regulation-21-1-c">
<Pnumber>c</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>parental leave,</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<Text>(referred to in paragraph (2) as a “statutory right") and also to a right which corresponds to that right and which arises under the employee’s contract of employment or otherwise.</Text>
</P2para>
</P2>
<P2 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/2" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/2" id="regulation-21-2">
<Pnumber>2</Pnumber>
<P2para>
<Text>In a case where this regulation applies—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/2/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/2/a" id="regulation-21-2-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>the employee may not exercise the statutory right and the corresponding right separately but may, in taking the leave for which the two rights provide, take advantage of whichever right is, in any particular respect, the more favourable, and</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/2/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/21/2/b" id="regulation-21-2-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>the provisions of the 1996 Act and of these Regulations relating to the statutory right apply, subject to any modifications necessary to give effect to any more favourable contractual terms, to the exercise of the composite right described in sub-paragraph (a) as they apply to the exercise of the statutory right.</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
</P2para>
</P2>
</P1para>
</P1>
</P1group>
<P1group RestrictStartDate="1999-12-15">
<Title> Calculation of a week’s pay</Title>
<P1 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/22" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/22" id="regulation-22">
<Pnumber>22</Pnumber>
<P1para>
<Text>Where—</Text>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/22/a" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/22/a" id="regulation-22-a">
<Pnumber>a</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>under Chapter II of part XIV of the 1996 Act, the amount of a week’s pay of an employee falls to be calculated by reference to the average rate of remuneration, or the average amount of remuneration, payable to the employee in respect of a period of twelve weeks ending on a particular date (referred to as “the calculation date");</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/22/b" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/22/b" id="regulation-22-b">
<Pnumber>b</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>during a week in that period, the employee was absent from work on ordinary or additional maternity leave or parental leave, and</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<P3 DocumentURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/22/c" IdURI="http://www.legislation.gov.uk/id/uksi/1999/3312/regulation/22/c" id="regulation-22-c">
<Pnumber>c</Pnumber>
<P3para>
<Text>remuneration is payable to the employee in respect of that week under her contract of employment, but the amount payable is less than the amount that would be payable if she were working,</Text>
</P3para>
</P3>
<Text>that week shall be disregarded for the purpose of the calculation and account shall be taken of remuneration in earlier weeks so as to bring up to twelve the number of weeks of which account is taken.</Text>
</P1para>
</P1>
</P1group>
</Part>
